<p align="center"><b>Munshi Nagar, Andheri (W), Mumbai-400058</b></p>
<p align="center"><b> Applied Sciences and Humanities Department</b></p>
<p align="center"><b>(2014-15)</b></p>
<p><b><span style="text-decoration: underline;">Course FEC105:  Basic Electrical and Electronics </span></b></p>
<p><b><span style="text-decoration: underline;">Course Education Objective:</span></b></p>
<ul>
<li><b>To introduce the concept of dc and ac circuit using various theorems and to apply it for circuit simplification.</b></li>
<li><b>To explain working principle, applications and construction of the single phase circuit, three phase circuit and transformer. </b></li>
<li><b>To explain construction, working and applications of basic electronic devices like diode and transistor.</b></li>
</ul>
<p><b><span style="text-decoration: underline;">Course Outcomes:</span></b></p>
